                ue.count(metricName, 1);             }                          //log metric for feature-analyzer             A.post(urlBase + "_popover_click", {});                          //log reftag for customer being shown quotes             var fitQuotes = $('.fit-recommendations-quote');                 });                                  A.post(urlQuotes + "_shown_" + fitQuotes.length);             }         });                  //We gather the number of counts for this feature being seen by user even if weblab gives this value.         if (typeof(ue) === 'object' && typeof(ue.count) ==='function') {             var metricName = "CustomerReviews:FitPop:aui:shown" + pipelineTreatment;             ue.count(metricName, 1);                          //log metric for feature-analyzer             A.post(urlBase + "_shown", {});         }                  $('#fitRecommendationsPopover').bind('touchmove', function(e) {           e.preventDefault();         ue.count(metricName, 1);     });       //This will submit a feedback to the server, it is generic that it can register any question and any answer     var submitFeedback = function(question, answer, retryLimit) {            var message = JSON.stringify([{question : question, answer : answer}]);              var params = {                     id                  : "DP-FitRecommendations-ajax",                     asin                : currentAsin,                     questionsAndAnswers : message,                     noCache             : A.now()                    };       var url = '/gp/customer-reviews/aj/fit-n-feel-experiment/submit-fit-feel-answer/ref=cm_cr_dp_fit_recommendations_';       url += (question == 'helpfulVote') ? 'vote' : 'comment';              var timeoutStart = 4000;       var submitWithRetries = function(params, attempts, retryLimit) {         //We need to retry at least 3 times, and each time try to add more time         retryLimit = retryLimit ? retryLimit : 3;         if (attempts > retryLimit) return;         var timeout = timeoutStart * attempts;         A.ajax(url, {                      method   : 'post',                       params   : params,                       timeout  : timeout,                      failure  : function() {                                   submitWithRetries(params, attempts + 1, retryLimit);;                                 }                     });       };       submitWithRetries(params, 1, retryLimit);     };      //Register the vote and then show the comments section     var vote = function(voteValue) {       //First lets ajax the vote and then show the thank you message       var answerText = voteValue ? 'yes' : 'no';       submitFeedback('helpfulVote', answerText, 3);       $('#fitRecommendationVoteSection').hide();       $('#fitRecommendationVoteThankYou').show(function() {         //Now we need to show the comments section         $('#fitRecommendationsCommentContainer').show({easing: 'swing', complete: function() {           $('#fitRecommendationsComment').focus();         }});       });     };      //We need to hook up the submit button to submit a comment and then update the UI     $('#fitRecommendationsCommentSubmit').bind('click', function() {       //First lets ajax the users comment                    function updateURLParameter(url, param, paramVal){             var newAdditionalURL = "";             var paramsArray = url.split("?");             var baseURL = paramsArray[0];             var additionalURL = paramsArray[1];             var urlParamDelimiter = "";             if (additionalURL) {                 paramsArray = additionalURL.split("&");                 var urlParamDelimiter + paramsArray[i];                         urlParamDelimiter = "&";                     }                 }             }              var modifiedParam = urlParamDelimiter + "" + param + "=" + paramVal;             return baseURL + "?" + newAdditionalURL + modifiedParam;         }                  function getIFrameHeight(){             var avail =  A.viewport().height - 300; with amazon prime student! I love the pants design and it looks just like the picture. The pants are so comfortable to as well and the material seems good so far! I'll update with more details once I start wearing them out.<br><br>I'm 5'11 to 6ft tall.<br><br> The only reason why i'm giving it a four stars is because I got the wrong size! I was kinda scared of getting the medium because  sometimes joggers pants can fit kinda snug and tight,but these are not like that at all. The are true to the sizing chart/info. I wear a 34 waist in jeans and a medium and jogging pants,but I have never had joggers before these pants.  I got some Allegra K men joggers from  amazon before and they were too tight,so that's why I went up a size this time around ,haha!<br><br>I will tell anybody please go by the sizing info if you're confused on what size to get, Its true to size. Don't get me wrong though,its not a huge difference. I guess if you love the kinda  into the semi baggy style than the large is for you. I just like my pants to fit a little snug and fitted.<br><br>I love these these southpole joggers and i will definitely order some more in a medium next time.<br><br>A little upadte: I tried them on with shoes and they look great overall! I might just order a large next time since there's not much of a difference. I'm kinda digging the loose fit look,haha!
